        }">TESTING</p>`);
        }

        preload(img_tour_url);
        get_product_json();
        var main_page = `<div class="main_page">
            <p>LOUIS VUITTON</p>
            <p>VR 全景空间体验</p>

            <button>探索更多 <img src='../vn_assets/subassets/LV/img/main_arrow.png' style="width: 16px;"></button>
        </div>`;
        var top_menu = `<img src='../vn_assets/subassets/LV/img/back_arrow2.png' class="back_arrow" style="display:none;">`;
        //<img src='../vn_assets/subassets/LV/img/icon/right_top.png' class="right_top">`;
        var mode_select_div = `<div class=mode_select_div>

        $('body').append(main_page);

            $('body').append(top_menu);
            var iframe = document.getElementById('showcase_iframe');
            $('.virtual_tour p').click(function(){
                if(_isload){
                    _isload = false;
                    iframe.src = _showcase_url;
                }else{
                    doorh();
                    get_product_json();
                }
                
                
               
                _mode = "v";
                $('.mode_select_div').hide();
                $('#container').css({"pointer-events":"all"});
                $(".back_arrow").show();
                
            });
            $('.image_tour p').click(function(){
                $('.mode_select_div').hide();
                _mode = "i";
                image_tour();
                $(".back_arrow").show();
            });
            $('.back_arrow').click(function(){
                /*$('.mode_select_div').remove();
                $('body').append(main_page);*/
                if(_mode == "v"){
                    if(_lv_lastmode == "mode.inside"){
                        lv_loading_bulid();
                        doorh();
                        if($('.rule_box').length > 0){
                            $('.rule_box').remove();
                        }
                    }
                    if(_lv_lastmode == "mode.dollhouse"){
                        $('.mode_select_div').show();
                        $('.doorh_title').remove();
                        $('.doorh_bottom').remove();
                        $('.lv_menu').hide();
                        //iframe.src = "";
                        get_product_json();
                        $(".back_arrow").hide();
                    }
                }

                if(_mode == "i"){
                    if($('.image_tour_div').is(":visible")){
                        $('.image_tour_div').remove();
                        $('.high_img_tour').remove();
                        $('.mode_select_div').show();
                        $(".back_arrow").hide();
                    }
                    if($('.high_img_tour').is(":visible")){
                        $('.image_tour_div').show();
                        $('.high_img_tour').hide();
                    }
                   
                }
                
            });
        });

       
        
      
    }
}

function sub_mapmove(e){
    console.log(e.sweep);
    console.log(e.position);
    console.log(e.rotation);
    _lastposit = e.position;
    _lv_lastrotate = e.rotation;
    var iframe = $('#showcase_iframe'); 
    if( $('#model-title',iframe.contents()).is(":visible")){
        $('#model-title',iframe.contents()).hide();
    }
    if(_lv_lastsweep !== e.sweep){
        _lv_lastsweep = e.sweep;
        $.each(area_sweep,function(k,v){
            if(v.sweep.includes(_lv_lastsweep)){
                _lastarea = lv_area_list[v.room];
                $('.min_tour span').html(_lastarea);
            }
        });
    }
    if(_lv_lastmode !== e.mode && e.mode !== "mode.transitioning"){
        _lv_lastmode = e.mode;
    }
    if(area_a.includes(e.sweep)){
        brightness_control("a");
    }else if(area_b.includes(e.sweep)){
        brightness_control("b");
    }else if(area_c.includes(e.sweep)){
        brightness_control("c");
    }else{
        brightness_control("d");
    }

    if(floorswitch){
        switch_floor(e.position);
    }else{
        if(JSON.stringify(_lastlvposit) !== JSON.stringify(e.position)){
            floorswitch = true;
        }
    }

    if(e.mode == "mode.inside"){
        if(_is_show_rule == "none"){
            _is_show_rule = true;
        }else{
            if(_is_show_rule){
                _is_show_rule = false;
                rule_box_bulid();
                rotate_div(e);
            }
        }
        if($(".product_billboard").length == 0 && !$('.menu_off').is(":visible")){
            $('.lv_menu').show();
            $('.lvmenu_on').show();
        }
        if($('.min_tour').length !== 0 && !$('.tour_div').is(":visible")){
            $('.min_tour').show();
        }
        rotate_div(e);
        
    }else{
        _mpSdk.Mattertag.getData()
        .then(function (e) {
            e.forEach(function (element) {
                _mpSdk.Mattertag.editOpacity(element['sid'], 0);
                _mpSdk.Mattertag.preventAction(element['sid'], {
                    opening: true
                });
            });
        });
        $('.rotate_div').remove();
        $('.lv_menu').hide();
        $('.menu_open').click();
        $('.menu_off').hide();
        $('.min_tour').hide();
        $('.tour_div').hide();
    }
    
}
function sub_mapphasechange(e){
    if (e.phase == 'appphase.playing'  ){
        if(_sid == "940U8"){
            const gui = new dat.GUI();

            gui.add( params, 'bness', 0, 3, 0.001 ).onChange( function ( value ) {
        
                $("#showcase_iframe").css({"filter":` brightness(${value}) contrast(${params.contrast}) grayscale(${params.grayscale}) saturate(${params.saturate})`});
        
            } );
            gui.add( params, 'contrast', 0, 3, 0.001 ).onChange( function ( value ) {
        
                $("#showcase_iframe").css({"filter":` brightness(${params.bness}) contrast(${value}) grayscale(${params.grayscale}) saturate(${params.saturate})`});
        
            } );
            gui.add( params, 'grayscale', 0, 1, 0.001 ).onChange( function ( value ) {
        
                $("#showcase_iframe").css({"filter":` brightness(${params.bness}) contrast(${params.contrast}) grayscale(${value}) saturate(${params.saturate})`});
        
            } );
            gui.add( params, 'saturate', 0, 3, 0.001 ).onChange( function ( value ) {
        
                $("#showcase_iframe").css({"filter":` brightness(${params.bness}) contrast(${params.contrast}) grayscale(${params.grayscale}) saturate(${value})`});
        
            } );
            gui.add( params, 'rotateY_range', 0, 100, 1 ).onChange( function ( value ) {

            } );
        };

        lv_loading_bulid();

        
        menu_bulid();
        get_tour_data();
        
        var dh_title = ``;
        //pointer_get_posit();
        //get_cam();
        registerIcon().then(()=> {
            bulid_tag();
            hide_matter_btn();
        });
        _mpSdk.on(_mpSdk.Sweep.Event.ENTER,
            function(oldSweep, newSweep){
                distancecal();
                if(_isautotour){
                    remove_lav_loading();
                }
            }
        );
        _mpSdk.on(_mpSdk.Mattertag.Event.CLICK, tagclick);
     
        _mpSdk.on(_mpSdk.Sweep.Event.EXIT, function(e){
            console.log('sweep EXIT');
            console.log(e);
            $('.rotate_min_div').hide();
            if(_isautotour){
                lv_loading_bulid();
            }
        });
    }
}

function bulid_tag(){
    _mpSdk.Mattertag.getData()
    .then((e) => {
        console.log(e);
        if(e.length !== 0){
            var new_lv_mtags_data = [];
            new_lv_mtags_data["nR38NJVnCca"] = [];
            new_lv_mtags_data["OpxEKcciRJH"] = [];
            new_lv_mtags_data["WlGtdNp2prr"] = [];
            changeicon1("nR38NJVnCca",1);
            changeicon1("OpxEKcciRJH",1);
            changeicon1("WlGtdNp2prr",1);
            var sku_list = ["R97094","M20067","R99967","N48105"];
            var sku_list2 = ["M23624", "M21222", "M21225", "M21226", "M21227", "M21228"];
            var sku_list3 = ["M23626","M47641","M20028","M21226","M12031","M20075"]; 
            e.forEach(element => {
                if (element['enabled']) {
                   
                    console.log(element['sid']);
                    if(element["label"] == "FERNANDO 与 HUMBERTO CAMPANA 设计的茧式吊椅"){
                        console.log(element["label"]);
                    }
                    $.each(_lv_mtags_data,function(k,v){
                        
                        if(element["label"] == v.Title){
                            if(v.Title == "FERNANDO 与 HUMBERTO CAMPANA 设计的茧式吊椅"){
                                console.log(v.Title);
                            }
                            new_lv_mtags_data[element["sid"]] = v; 
                            if(v.TAG == "H"){
                                changeicon(element['sid'],1);
                            }
                            if(v.TAG == "B"){
                                changeicon1(element['sid'],1);
                            }
                        }
                        if(v.hasOwnProperty('SKU')){
                            if(sku_list.includes(v.SKU)){
                                new_lv_mtags_data["nR38NJVnCca"].push(v);
                                var index = sku_list.indexOf(v.SKU);
                                sku_list.splice(index, 1);
                            }
                            if(sku_list2.includes(v.SKU)){
                                new_lv_mtags_data["OpxEKcciRJH"].push(v);
                                var index = sku_list2.indexOf(v.SKU);
                                sku_list2.splice(index, 1);
                            }
                            if(sku_list3.includes(v.SKU)){
                                new_lv_mtags_data["WlGtdNp2prr"].push(v);
                                var index = sku_list3.indexOf(v.SKU);
                                sku_list3.splice(index, 1);
                            }
                        }
                        
                    });
                   
                        
                     
                    if(Math.abs(_lastposit['x'] - element["anchorPosition"]['x']) < distance && Math.abs(_lastposit['z'] - element["anchorPosition"]['z']) < distance){
                        element['posit'] = false;
                    }else{
                        element['posit'] = true;
                    }
                    if(element['posit']){
                        _mpSdk.Mattertag.editOpacity(element['sid'], 0);
                        _mpSdk.Mattertag.preventAction(element['sid'], {
                            opening: true,
                        });
                    }
                }
            });
            console.log("_lv_mtags_data67");
            console.log(new_lv_mtags_data);
            _lv_mtags_data = new_lv_mtags_data;
            
        }
        _lv_mtags = e;
    })
}

function get_cam(){
    _mpSdk.Camera.pose.subscribe(e=>{

        _camerapose  = e;

        if (e.mode == "mode.dollhouse"){
            bulid_blockbutton();

        }else{
            $('.block').remove();
        }


    })
}

function bulid_blockbutton(){
    if($('.block').length == 0){
        var blockbutton_div =``;
        $.each(blockbutton,function(k,v){
            /*blockbutton_div += `<div class='block ${v.name}'>
            <div class="bubble">${v.name}</div>
            <div class="bubble_pointer"></div>
            </div>`;*/
            blockbutton_div += `<div class='block ${v.name}'>
                <div class="dialog-border-${v.type}">${v.name}</div>
            </div>`
        });
        $('#container').append(blockbutton_div);
    }
    blockbutton_control();
}

function blockbutton_control(){
    var showcase = document.getElementById('showcase_iframe');
    var showcaseSize = {
        w: showcase.clientWidth,
        h: showcase.clientHeight,
    };

    $.each(blockbutton,function(k,v){
        var blockId = $(`.${v.name}`);

        var screenCoordinate = _mpSdk.Conversion.worldToScreen(v.posit, _camerapose, showcaseSize)
        if ((screenCoordinate.x<=0 && screenCoordinate.y<=0) || (screenCoordinate.x>0 && screenCoordinate.y>0)  ){

            var left = Math.abs(screenCoordinate.x) - 11
            var top = Math.abs(screenCoordinate.y) - 50
        
            blockId.css("left",left)
            blockId.css("top",top)
        }
        else{

            blockId.css("left",-100)
            blockId.css("top",-100)
        }

    });
}

function registerIcon(){
    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
        _mpSdk.Mattertag.registerIcon('o', 'https://l2vr.co/vn_assets/subassets/LV/img/icon/product_tag.png');
        _mpSdk.Mattertag.registerIcon('f', 'https://l2vr.co/vn_assets/subassets/LV/img/f_tag_icon.png');
        /*for (var i = 0; i < 29; i++) {
            _mpSdk.Mattertag.registerIcon(`t${i}`, `https://l2vr.co/vn_assets/subassets/LV/img/tag/tag-${i}.png`);
        }*/
       
        resolve();
    });
}

function switch_floor(position){
    $.each(floor,function(k,v){
        if(JSON.stringify(position) == JSON.stringify(v.position)){
            console.log(position)
            console.log("params.floor_effect_FLY");
            console.log(params.floor_effect_FLY);
            if(params.floor_effect_FLY){
                var transition = _mpSdk.Sweep.Transition.FLY;
            }else{
                var transition = _mpSdk.Sweep.Transition.INSTANT;
            }
            
            var transitionTime = 6000; // in milliseconds
            var f = k;
            console.log(k)
            if(k == "1"){
                f = "4"
            }else{
                f = "1"
            }
            
            lv_loading_bulid();

            _lastlvposit = floor[f].position;
            _mpSdk.Sweep.moveTo(floor[f].sweep, {
                rotation: floor[f].rotation,
                transition: transition,
                transitionTime: transitionTime,
            })
            .then(function(sweepId){
                floorswitch = false;
                setTimeout(function(){
                    remove_lav_loading();
                },1000)
            })
            .catch(function(error){
                // Error with moveTo command
                console.log(error);
            });
            
        }
    })
    
}

function brightness_control(area){
    if(area == "d"){
        $("#showcase_iframe").css({"filter":` brightness(1.13)`});
    }
    if(area == "c"){
        $("#showcase_iframe").css({"filter":` brightness(0.937) contrast(1) saturate(1.02)`});
    }
    if(area == "b"){
        $("#showcase_iframe").css({"filter":` brightness(1.2) contrast(1) saturate(1)`});
    }
    if(area == "a"){
        $("#showcase_iframe").css({"filter":` brightness(0.95) contrast(1) saturate(1)`});
    }
}

function distancecal(){
    $.each(_lv_mtags, (index, tag) => {
     
        if(Math.abs(_lastposit['x'] - tag.anchorPosition['x']) < distance && Math.abs(_lastposit['z'] - tag.anchorPosition['z']) < distance){
            _lv_mtags[index]['posit'] = false;
        }else{
            _lv_mtags[index]['posit'] = true;
        }
        
        if(_lv_mtags[index]['posit']){
            
            _mpSdk.Mattertag.preventAction(tag.sid, {
                opening: true,
            });
            _mpSdk.Mattertag.editOpacity(tag.sid, 0);
            var stemVector = { x: 0, y: 0, z: 0 }

            
            _mpSdk.Mattertag.editPosition(tag.sid, { stemVector: stemVector, anchorPosition: tag.anchorPosition })
            .then((e) => {
    
            })
            
        }else{
            if(tag.exclude == 0){
                _mpSdk.Mattertag.editOpacity(tag.sid, parseInt(_isInvisibleTag)/100);
            }else{
                _mpSdk.Mattertag.editOpacity(tag.sid, 1);
            }  
            _mpSdk.Mattertag.editPosition(tag.sid, { stemVector: tag.stemVector, anchorPosition: tag.anchorPosition })
            .then((e) => {
    
            })
        }

    });
}

    console.log('hide_matter_btn');
    if($(window).width() <= 600){
        console.log('iframe67')
        var iframe = $('#showcase_iframe'); 
        console.log($('.bottom-controls', iframe.contents()));
        $('.bottom-controls', iframe.contents()).hide();
        //$('.bottom-ui', iframe.contents()).hide();
        $('#footer span', iframe.contents()).hide();
        $('.footer-ui', iframe.contents()).hide();
        $('#model-title',iframe.contents()).hide();
        setTimeout(function(){
            console.log('iframe67')
            $('.bottom-controls', iframe.contents()).hide();
            console.log($('.bottom-controls', iframe.contents()));
            //$('.bottom-ui', iframe.contents()).hide();
            $('#footer span', iframe.contents()).hide();
            $('.footer-ui', iframe.contents()).hide();
            $('#model-title',iframe.contents()).hide();
        }, 1500)
    }
}

function menu_bulid(){
    var vr = new vr_mode();
 
    var menu_div = //<img src='../vn_assets/subassets/LV/img/icon/menu_base.png' class="menu_off">
    `<div class="lv_menu">
        <img src='../vn_assets/subassets/LV/img/icon/menu_off.png' class="menu_off">
        <div class="lvmenu_on">
            <img src='../vn_assets/subassets/LV/img/icon/product.png' class="product">
            <p>产品</p>
            <img src='../vn_assets/subassets/LV/img/icon/auto.png' data-status="off" class="auto" style="height:5.8vw">
            <p>自动导览</p>
            ${_isMobile ? `<img src='../vn_assets/subassets/LV/img/icon/motion.png' data-status="off" class="motion"><p>重力感应</p>` : ""}
            <img src='../vn_assets/subassets/LV/img/icon/menu_open.png' class="menu_open">
        </div>
    </div>`;
    $('body').append(menu_div);
    
    $('.menu_off').click(function(){
        $('.menu_off').slideUp();
        $('.lvmenu_on').slideDown( "slow", function() {
            // Animation complete.
            
        }); 
    });

    $('.menu_open').click(function(){

        $('.menu_off').show();
        $('.lvmenu_on').slideUp( "slow", function() {
            
        });

    });

    $('.product').click(function(){
        product_list(_lv_mtags_data);
        $('.auto').attr("src","../vn_assets/subassets/LV/img/icon/auto.png");
        $('.motion').attr("src","../vn_assets/subassets/LV/img/icon/motion.png");
    });

    $('.auto').click(function(){
        if($('.auto').data('status') == "off"){
            $('.auto').attr("src","../vn_assets/subassets/LV/img/icon/autoing.png");
            $('.motion').attr("src","../vn_assets/subassets/LV/img/icon/motion.png");
            $('.auto').data('status',"on");
            if($('.min_tour').is(":visible")){
                $('.min_tour').click();
            }
            auto_tour();
        }else{
            _mpSdk.Tour.stop();
            $('.auto').attr("src","../vn_assets/subassets/LV/img/icon/auto.png");
            $('.motion').attr("src","../vn_assets/subassets/LV/img/icon/motion.png");
            $('.auto').data('status',"off");
            if($('.tour_div').is(":visible")){
                $('.close_tour').click();
            }
        }   
        
    });
    
    $('.motion').click(function(){
        if($('#panoSet').length == 0){
            $('.auto').attr("src","../vn_assets/subassets/LV/img/icon/auto.png");
            $('.motion').attr("src","../vn_assets/subassets/LV/img/icon/motioning.png");
            $('.motion').data('status',"on");
            if(!_isIPhone){
                vr.view360();
            }else{
                vr.new_vr()
            }
        }else{
            console.log(vr.panoViewer);
            $('.auto').attr("src","../vn_assets/subassets/LV/img/icon/auto.png");
            $('.motion').attr("src","../vn_assets/subassets/LV/img/icon/motion.png");
            $('.motion').data('status',"off");
            vr.panoViewer.destroy();
            $('#panoSet').remove();
            vr.panoViewer = "";
        }
    });

    _mpSdk.Camera.pose.subscribe(function (e) {
        vr._y = e.rotation.y;
        vr._x = e.rotation.x;
    });
}

function product_billboard_bulid(id){

            console.log(area)
            if(area < label_json.length){
                if (!ct.getCookie(label_json[area].name)) {
                    ct.setCookie(label_json[area].name,true,30)
                }
            }
    
        }
        console.log(_lv_mtags_data[id]);

        console.log(typeof _lv_mtags_data[id]);
        if(_lv_mtags_data[id].hasOwnProperty('No.')){

                _img_tour_pointer = area_name[area_name.length-1];
                console.log(url)

                    $('.tag').remove();
                    $('.backImg').attr("src", `${url}`);
                    $('.c_img').css({"background-image": `url(${img_tour_url[low_pointer]})`});

                        `${url}`,

            console.log(product_data.iv_url_low);

                    })

                        console.log(product_data.iv_url_low.length)
                        if(pointer < product_data.iv_url_low.length-1){

                <img class="product_close_icon" src="../vn_assets/subassets/LV/img/icon/close_base.png">

            <div class="product_billboard_body">`;
            $.each(product_list,function(k,v){
                if(typeof v !== "undefined"){
                    if(v.hasOwnProperty("iv_url_low")){
                        if(typeof v.iv_url_low == "object"){
                            product_bb += `<div class="product_media_block" style="display:block;position: relative;">`;
                            
                            product_bb += `<img class="media_img" src="${v.iv_url_low[0]}"></img><span data-key="${k}">查看详情</span>`;
            
                            product_bb += `</div>`;

                    }

                        product_bb += `<p class="product_title">${v.Title}</p>`;
                    }
                }
               
            });

            product_bb += `</div>
            </div>`;
            $('body').append(product_bb);
            $('.lv_menu').hide();
            $('.menu_off').hide();
            $('.product_close_div').click(function(){
                
                $('.product_billboard').remove();
                $('.lv_menu').show();
                $('.lvmenu_on').show();
            });

            $('.product_media_block span').click(function(){
                var product_data = product_list[$(this).data("key")];
                $('.product_billboard_body').html();
                var product_bb = ``;
                if(product_data.hasOwnProperty("iv_url_low")){
                    if(typeof product_data.iv_url_low == "object"){
                        product_bb += `<div class="product_media_block">
                        <img class="left_arrow" src="../vn_assets/subassets/LV/img/icon/left_arrow.png">`

                        product_bb += `<img class="media_img" src="${product_data.iv_url_low[0]}"></img>`;
        
                        product_bb += `<img class="right_arrow" src="../vn_assets/subassets/LV/img/icon/right_arrow.png">
                        </div>`;
                    }
                }
               
                if(product_data.hasOwnProperty("SKU")){
                    product_bb += `<p class="product_sku">${product_data.SKU}</p>`;
                }
                if(product_data.hasOwnProperty("Title")){
                    product_bb += `<p class="product_title">${product_data.Title}</p>`;
                }
                product_bb += `<p class="product_line"><i class="fa fa-minus" aria-hidden="true"></i></p>`;
                if(product_data.hasOwnProperty("Price")){
                    product_bb += `<p class="product_price">${product_data.Price}</p>`;
                }
                if(product_data.hasOwnProperty("Description")){
                    product_bb += `<p class="product_desc" style="margin-bottom: 3vh;">${product_data.Description}</p>`;
                }
                if(product_data.hasOwnProperty("pdp_url")){
                    product_bb += `<button>前往选购</button>`;
                }

                $('.product_billboard_body').html(product_bb);
                if(typeof product_data.iv_url_low == "object"){
                    if(product_data.iv_url_low.length <= 1){
                        $('.left_arrow').hide();
                        $('.right_arrow').hide();
                        $('.product_media_block').css("display","block");
                    }else{
                        var pointer = 0;
                        $('.left_arrow').click(function(){
                            if(pointer > 0){
                                pointer--;
                                $('.media_img').attr('src',product_data.iv_url_low[pointer]);
                            }else{
                                pointer = product_data.iv_url_low.length -1;
                                $('.media_img').attr('src',product_data.iv_url_low[pointer]);
                            }
                            console.log(pointer)
                            console.log(product_data.iv_url_low[pointer])
                        })
            
                        $('.right_arrow').click(function(){
                            if(pointer < product_data.iv_url_low.length){
                                pointer++;
                                $('.media_img').attr('src',product_data.iv_url_low[pointer]);
                            }else{
                                pointer = 0;
                                $('.media_img').attr('src',product_data.iv_url_low[pointer]);
                            }
                        });
                    }
                  
                }
                $('.product_billboard_body button').click(function(){
                    if(product_data.hasOwnProperty("pdp_url")){
                        if(product_data.hasOwnProperty("Title")){
                            var action = `Product - Enter (${product_data.Title}-${product_data.pdp_url})`;
                        }else{
                            var action = `Product - Enter (${product_data.pdp_url})`;
                        }
                        gasubmitevent(action);
                        if(_ismin == 1){
                            jumpToMiniProgram(product_data.SPU,product_data.SKU);
                        }else{
                            window.open(product_data.pdp_url, '_blank');
                        }
                    }
                });
            });
        }

       
    }
}

function product_list(pl_data){
    console.log("pl_data67")
    console.log(pl_data)
    $('.back_arrow').hide();
    var product_list = `<div class="product_list">
    <img src='../vn_assets/subassets/LV/img/back_arrow.png' class="product_list_back_arrow">
    <p class="product_list_title">产品列表</p>
    <div class="product_list_button_list">`;
    $.each(lv_area_list,function(k,v){
        product_list += `<button data-sort="${k}">${v}</button>`;
    });

    product_list += `</div>`;
    product_list += `<div class="product_list_block">`;
    for (var key in pl_data) {
        if (pl_data.hasOwnProperty(key)) {
            console.log(pl_data[key]);
            if(pl_data[key].hasOwnProperty('No.')){
                var img_url ;
                if(typeof pl_data[key].iv_url_low == "string"){
                    img_url = pl_data[key].iv_url_low;
                }
                if(typeof pl_data[key].iv_url_low == "object"){
                    img_url = pl_data[key].iv_url_low[0];
                }
                product_list += `<div class="product_data" data-type="${pl_data[key].Area}">
                
                <button data-key="${key}"><img src="${img_url}"><span>查看详情</span></button>`;
                if(pl_data[key].hasOwnProperty("SKU")){
                    product_list +=  `<p>${pl_data[key].SKU}</p>`;
                }
                product_list += `<hr class="">
                <p>${pl_data[key].Title}</p>
                </div>
                `;
            }else{
                console.log(key)
                console.log(pl_data[key])
                $.each(pl_data[key],function(k,v){
                    if(typeof v !== "undefined"){
                        var img_url ;
                    
                        if(typeof v.iv_url_low == "string"){
                            img_url = v.iv_url_low;
                        }
                        if(typeof v.iv_url_low == "object"){
                            img_url = v.iv_url_low[0];
                        }
                        product_list += `<div class="product_data" data-type="${v.Area}">
                        
                        <button data-key="${key}"><img src="${img_url}"><span>查看详情</span></button>`;
                        if(v.hasOwnProperty("SKU")){
                            product_list +=  `<p>${v.SKU}</p>`;
                        }
                        product_list += `<hr class="">
                        <p>${v.Title}</p>
                        </div>
                        `;
                    }
                    
                });
            }
        }
    }
    product_list += `</div>`;


    product_list += `</div>`;

    $('body').append(product_list);
    $('.product_list_button_list button').eq(6).html(lv_area_list[7])
    $('.product_list_button_list button').eq(7).html(lv_area_list[6])
    $('.product_data button').click(function(){
        
        if($('.high_img_tour').length == 0){
            //product_billboard_bulid($(this).data("key"));
            console.log($(this).data("key"))
            var tag_sid = $(this).data("key");
            lv_loading_bulid();
            if(tag_sid !== "nR38NJVnCca"){
                _mpSdk.Mattertag.navigateToTag(`${tag_sid}`, _mpSdk.Mattertag.Transition.FLY)
                .then(function () {
                    console.log("navigateToTag done")
                    distancecal();
                    _mpSdk.Camera.setRotation({ x: 0, y: _lv_lastrotate.y }, { speed: 180 })
                    .then(function() {
                        // Camera rotation complete.
                        remove_lav_loading();
                    })
                    .catch(function(error) {
                        // Camera rotation error.
                    });
                });
            }else{
                const sweepId = "b48857056cf34d2a9b2b4e5f5e357151"
                const rotation = {x: 7.041580982699085, y: -153.05361967867077};
                const transition = _mpSdk.Sweep.Transition.FLY;
                const transitionTime = 1000; // in milliseconds

                _mpSdk.Sweep.moveTo(sweepId, {
                    rotation: rotation,
                    transition: transition,
                    transitionTime: transitionTime,
                })
                .then(function(sweepId){
                    // Move successful.
                    console.log('Arrived at sweep ' + sweepId);
                    remove_lav_loading();
                })
                .catch(function(error){
                    // Error with moveTo command
                });
            }
            
            $('.back_arrow').show();
            $('.product_list').remove();
        }else{
            var tag_sid = $(this).data("key");
            console.log($(this).data("key"))
            var no = $(this).data("key");
            console.log(no);
            product_billboard_bulid(no);
            $('.back_arrow').show();
            $('.product_list').remove();
        }
        
    });
    $('.product_list_back_arrow').click(function(){
        $('.back_arrow').show();
        $('.product_list').remove();
    })

    $('.product_list_button_list button').click(function(){
        $('.product_list_button_list button').css({ '-webkit-box-shadow':'0 0 0px ivory',
        '-moz-box-shadow': '0 0 0px ivory', 
        'box-shadow':'0 0 0px ivory',});
        $(this).css({ '-webkit-box-shadow':'0 0 10px ivory',
            '-moz-box-shadow': '0 0 10px ivory', 
            'box-shadow':'0 0 10px ivory',});
        console.log($(this).data("sort"));
        var sort = $(this).data("sort");
        console.log(sort)
      
        if(sort == 0){
            $('.product_data').show();
        }else{
            $.each($('.product_data'),function(k,v){
                if($('.product_data').eq(k).data('type') !== sort) {
                    $('.product_data').eq(k).hide();
                }else{
                    $('.product_data').eq(k).show();
                }
            });
        }
        if(sort !== 0){
            if(low_pointer !== sort-1){
                low_pointer = sort-1;
                console.log(low_pointer)
                hight_pointer = 0;
                if($('.backImg').length == 1){
                    $('.tag').remove();
                    console.log(low_pointer)
                    console.log(image_tour_data_low)
                    console.log(image_tour_data_low[low_pointer])
                    var url = image_tour_data_low[low_pointer][hight_pointer];
                    var area_name = url.split('/');
                    _img_tour_pointer = area_name[area_name.length-1];

                    $('.backImg').attr("src", `${url}`);
                    $('.c_img').css({"background-image": `url(${img_tour_url[low_pointer]})`});
                    getMeta(
                        `${url}`,
                        (width, height) => { 
                            
                            if($(window).width() < 1024){
                                $('.backImg_div').css({"margin-top":`${($(window).height() -$('.backImg').height())/2 }px`}) 
                            }else{
                                $('.backImg_div').css({"margin-top":`${($(window).height() -$('.backImg').height())/2 }px` , "margin-left":`${($(window).width() -$('.backImg').width())/2 }px`}) 
                            }
                            if(tag_poist.hasOwnProperty(_img_tour_pointer)){
                                bulid_img_tag(tag_poist[_img_tour_pointer]);
                            }
                    }
                    );
                    if(low_pointer == 6){
                        $('.area_title').html(lv_area_list[low_pointer]);
                        $('.high_area_title').html(lv_area_list[low_pointer]);
                    }else if(low_pointer == 5){
                        $('.area_title').html(lv_area_list[7]);
                        $('.high_area_title').html(lv_area_list[7]);
                    }else{
                        $('.area_title').html(lv_area_list[low_pointer+1]);
                        $('.high_area_title').html(lv_area_list[low_pointer+1]);
                    }
                    
                    $('.area_title_cn').html(lv_area_list_cn[low_pointer]);
                    img_all_product_controll(low_pointer);
                }
            }
            
        }
    })
}

function control_rotation(e){
    if(e.rotation.x > 10 || e.rotation.x < -10){
        _mpSdk.Camera.setRotation({ x: 0, y: e.rotation.y }, { speed: 180 })
        .then(function() {
            // Camera rotation complete.
        })
        .catch(function(error) {
            // Camera rotation error.
        });
    }
}

function get_tour_data(){
    console.log(_mpSdk.Tour)
    var Tour = _mpSdk.Tour;
    
    _mpSdk.on(Tour.Event.STEPPED, function(tourIndex){
        remove_lav_loading();
        console.log('Tour index ' + tourIndex);
        
        console.log(_tour_snapshots[tourIndex]);
        
        if($('.tour').length !== 0){
            $.each(lv_area_list,function(k,v){
                if(_tour_snapshots[tourIndex].name == v){
                    _last_tour_key = k -1;
                    $('.tour').find("img").css({'-webkit-box-shadow':'0 0 0px ivory',
                    '-moz-box-shadow': '0 0 0px ivory',
                    'box-shadow':'0 0 0px ivory',
                    'border':'0px solid #fff'});

                    $('.tour').eq(_last_tour_key).find("img").css({'-webkit-box-shadow':'0 0 8px ivory',
                        '-moz-box-shadow': '0 0 8px ivory',
                        'box-shadow':'0 0 8px ivory',
                        'border':'1px solid #fff'});

                    var leftposit = _last_tour_key * ($(window).width() * 0.29333);
                    $('.tour_list').scrollLeft( leftposit )
                }
                
            })
        }
    
    });
    _mpSdk.on(Tour.Event.STARTED, function(){
        console.log('Tour started');
        $('.auto').attr("src","../vn_assets/subassets/LV/img/icon/autoing.png");
        $('.motion').attr("src","../vn_assets/subassets/LV/img/icon/motion.png");
        $('.rotate_min_div').hide();
        _isautotour = true;
    });
    _mpSdk.on(Tour.Event.STOPPED, function(){
        console.log('Tour stopped');
        $('.auto').attr("src","../vn_assets/subassets/LV/img/icon/auto.png");
        $('.motion').attr("src","../vn_assets/subassets/LV/img/icon/motion.png");
        _isautotour = false;
    });
    _mpSdk.Tour.getData()
    .then(function(snapshots) {
        // Tour getData complete.
        _tour_snapshots = snapshots;
    })
    .catch(function(error) {
        // Tour getData error.
    });
}

function tour_control(){
    console.log(_tour_snapshots);
    var min_tour_button = `<div class="min_tour">`;
    //<img class="room_arrow" src="../vn_assets/subassets/LV/img/room_arrow.png">
    min_tour_button += `<img class="min_img" src="../vn_assets/subassets/LV/img/icon/path_arrow2.png">
    <span>${_lastarea}</span>
    </div>`;

    var tour_div = `<div class="tour_div" style="display:none;">
        <p class="title">切换房间</p>
        <div class="close_tour">
            <span>收起</span>
            <img src="../vn_assets/subassets/LV/img/icon/path_arrow.png">
        </div>
        <div class="tour_list">`;
        console.log(lv_area_list.length);
        var array_key = 0;
        $.each(_tour_snapshots,function(k,v){
            
            console.log(v.name.length);
            if(v.name.length > 0){
                tour_div += `<div class="tour" data-key="${k}">`
                
                if(v.name == "Malle Vendome"){
                    tour_div += `<img src="https://hardsided.lvcampaign.com/attached/lvtrunk/tour/ChangeRoomsCarousel/07.png">`;
                    tour_div += `<p>${lv_area_list_cn["6"]}</p>`
                }else
                if(v.name == "High Tea Trunk"){
                    tour_div += `<img src="https://hardsided.lvcampaign.com/attached/lvtrunk/tour/ChangeRoomsCarousel/06.png">`;
                    tour_div += `<p>${lv_area_list_cn["5"]}</p>`
                    
                    
                }else{
                    tour_div += `<img src="https://hardsided.lvcampaign.com/attached/lvtrunk/tour/ChangeRoomsCarousel/0${array_key+1}.jpg">`;
                    tour_div += `<p>${lv_area_list_cn[array_key]}</p>`
                }
                
                
                tour_div +=`</div>`;
                array_key++;
            }
        });
        tour_div += `</div>
    </div>`;

    $('body').append(min_tour_button);

    $('.min_tour').click(function(){
        $('.rotate_min_div').hide();
        $('.min_tour').slideUp();
        if($('.tour_div').length == 0){
            $('body').append(tour_div);
            $('.tour_div').slideDown();
            $('.close_tour').click(function(){
                $('.tour_div').slideUp();
                $('.min_tour').slideDown();
            });
            $('.tour').click(function(){
                _mpSdk.Tour.stop();
                console.log($(this).data("key"));
                $('.tour').find("img").css({'-webkit-box-shadow':'0 0 0px ivory',
                '-moz-box-shadow': '0 0 0px ivory',
                'box-shadow':'0 0 0px ivory',
                'border':'0px solid #fff'});

                $(this).find("img").css({'-webkit-box-shadow':'0 0 8px ivory',
                    '-moz-box-shadow': '0 0 8px ivory',
                    'box-shadow':'0 0 8px ivory',
                    'border':'1px solid #fff'});
                _mpSdk.Tour.step($(this).data("key"));
                
            });
        }else{
            $('.tour_div').slideDown();
        }
        

    });
}

function auto_tour(){
   
    _mpSdk.Tour.start(_last_tour_key)
    .then(function() {
        // Tour start complete.
        _last_tour_key = 0;
    })
    .catch(function(error) {
        // Tour start error.
    });
}

            new_lv_mtags_data[32][v["No."]]= v;

            new_lv_mtags_data[v["No."]] = v;
        }

            img_tag_data[v.photo_ablum_url_low.split('/')[v.photo_ablum_url_low.split('/').length -1]+"-"+v['No.']] = v;
        }
       
        
    });
    _lv_mtags_data = new_lv_mtags_data;
    console.log(_lv_mtags_data);
    $.each(image_tour_data_low,function(k,v){
        preload(v);
        $.each(v,function(vk,vv){

            img_data.push(vv);
        });
    })
    var image_tour_div = `<div class="image_tour_div">

                    margin-right: 2.133vw;width:3.667vw;"></img>

    $('.c3').css({'left':`${($('.c2').width() - $('.c3').width()-2)/2}px`,"top":`${($('.c2').width() - $('.c3').width()-2)/2}px`});
    $('.c4').css({'left':`${($('.c3').width() - $('.c4').width()-2)/2}px`,"top":`${($('.c3').width() - $('.c4').width()-2)/2}px`});
    $('.c_img').css({'left':`${($('.c4').width() - $('.c_img').width())/2}px`,"top:":`${($('.c4').width() - $('.c_img').width())/2}px`});

    $('.img_right_arrow').css({"margin-top":`${$('.c3').width()/2 - $('.img_right_arrow').height()/2}px`});
    $('.c_img').css({"background-image": "url(https://hardsided.lvcampaign.com/attached/lvtrunk/tour/ChangeRoomsCarousel/01.jpg)"});

                            <div class="backImg_div">
                                <img class="backImg" src="https://hardsided.lvcampaign.com/attached/lvtrunk/tour/GZHS2/${img_folder}/${_img_tour_pointer}">

    `;

    $('body').append(high_img_tour);
    var startT = 0, endT = false,startX = 0 ,endX = 0;;
    $(".high_img_tour").on("touchstart",function(e){
        console.log(e)
        startT = e.timeStamp;
        startX = e.touches[0].pageX;
    });
    $(".high_img_tour").on("touchmove",function(e){
        //console.log(e)
        /*if(startT){
            startT = false;
            startX = e.touches[0].pageX;
            console.log(startX)
        }*/
        endX = e.touches[0].pageX;
    });
    $(".high_img_tour").on("touchend touchcancel",function(e){
       
        if(e.timeStamp - startT > 150){
            console.log(e)
            if(startX > endX){
                $('.high_right_arrow').click();
            }else{
                $('.high_left_arrow').click();
            }
        }
        
    });
    img_all_product_controll(0);

function img_all_product_controll(area){
    area++;
    var product_number = 0;
    $.each(_lv_mtags_data,function(k,v){
        if(v.Area == area){
            product_number ++;
        }
    });
    $('.high_img_tour button').html(`全部商品 ${product_number}`)
    $('.high_img_tour button').unbind( "click" );
    $('.high_img_tour button').click(function(){
        product_list(_lv_mtags_data);
        $('.product_list_button_list button').eq(area).click();
    });
    
}

function bulid_img_tag(tag_list){
    
    if($('.high_img_tour').length > 0){
        console.log('bulid_img_tag67')
        var list_data = {};
        var area = _lv_mtags_data[tag_list[0].no].Area
        var product_number = 0;
        $.each(_lv_mtags_data,function(k,v){
            if(v.Area == area){
                product_number ++;
            }
        });
        $.each(tag_list,function(k,v){
            console.log(v)
            list_data[v.no] = _lv_mtags_data[v.no];
            var tag_div = `<img class="tag" src="https://l2vr.co/vn_assets/subassets/LV/img/icon/product_tag.png" data-no="${v.no}" style="position: absolute;top:${v.top};left:${v.left};width:8vw;">`;
            if($(window).width() < 1024){
                $('.high_img_tour').append(tag_div);
            }else{
                $('.backImg_div').append(tag_div)
            }
            

        });
        $('.tag').click(function(){
            console.log($(this).data("no"));
            product_billboard_bulid($(this).data("no"));
        });
    }else{
        $('.high_img_tour button').hide();
    }
}

function rotate_div(cam_data){
    if(!_isautotour){
        var tour_a_array = [1,4,5,8,13,16,14];
        if(rotate_block_data.hasOwnProperty(cam_data.sweep) && $('.min_tour').is(":visible")){
            //console.log(cam_data.rotation.y - rotate_block_data[cam_data.sweep].rotation.y)
            if(cam_data.rotation.y - rotate_block_data[cam_data.sweep].rotation.y <= 10 &&  cam_data.rotation.y - rotate_block_data[cam_data.sweep].rotation.y >= -10){
               
                var rotate_min_div = `<div class="rotate_min_div">
                    <span>${lv_area_list[rotate_block_data[cam_data.sweep].connect_area]}</span>`;
                if(rotate_block_data[cam_data.sweep].connect_area == 6){
                    rotate_min_div += `<img src="https://hardsided.lvcampaign.com/attached/lvtrunk/tour/ChangeRoomsCarousel/06.png">`;
                    
                }else if(rotate_block_data[cam_data.sweep].connect_area == 7){
                    rotate_min_div += `<img src="https://hardsided.lvcampaign.com/attached/lvtrunk/tour/ChangeRoomsCarousel/07.png">`;
                }else{
                    rotate_min_div += `<img src="https://hardsided.lvcampaign.com/attached/lvtrunk/tour/ChangeRoomsCarousel/0${rotate_block_data[cam_data.sweep].connect_area}.jpg">`;
                }
                rotate_min_div +=`</div>`;
                if($('.rotate_min_div').length == 0){
                    $('body').append(rotate_min_div)
                    $('.rotate_min_div').click(function(){
                        /*var areadata = label_json[rotate_block_data[cam_data.sweep].connect_area -1]
                        const sweepId = areadata.start_sweep;
                        const rotation = areadata.rotation;
                        const transition = _mpSdk.Sweep.Transition.INSTANT;
                        const transitionTime = 2000; // in milliseconds
    
                        _mpSdk.Sweep.moveTo(sweepId, {
                            rotation: rotation,
                            transition: transition,
                            transitionTime: transitionTime,
                        })
                        .then(function(sweepId){
                            // Move successful.
                            console.log('Arrived at sweep ' + sweepId);
                        })
                        .catch(function(error){
                            // Error with moveTo command
                        });*/
                        console.log(rotate_block_data[cam_data.sweep].connect_area);
                        var a = parseInt(rotate_block_data[cam_data.sweep].connect_area);
                        
                        _mpSdk.Tour.step(tour_a_array[a-1]);
                    });
                }else{
                    
                    if(!$('.rotate_min_div').is(":visible")){
                        $('.rotate_min_div span').html(lv_area_list[rotate_block_data[cam_data.sweep].connect_area])
                        if(rotate_block_data[cam_data.sweep].connect_area == 6){
                            $('.rotate_min_div img').attr('src',`https://hardsided.lvcampaign.com/attached/lvtrunk/tour/ChangeRoomsCarousel/06.png`);
                        }else if(rotate_block_data[cam_data.sweep].connect_area == 7){
                            $('.rotate_min_div img').attr('src',`https://hardsided.lvcampaign.com/attached/lvtrunk/tour/ChangeRoomsCarousel/07.png`);
                        }else{
                            $('.rotate_min_div img').attr('src',`https://hardsided.lvcampaign.com/attached/lvtrunk/tour/ChangeRoomsCarousel/0${rotate_block_data[cam_data.sweep].connect_area}.jpg`);              
                        }
                    }
                    $('.rotate_min_div').show();
                    
                }
            }else{
                $('.rotate_min_div').hide();
                $('.rotate_min_div span').html('')
                $('.rotate_min_div img').attr('src','');
            }
            
            
        }
    }else{
        $('.rotate_min_div').hide();
        $('.rotate_min_div span').html('')
        $('.rotate_min_div img').attr('src','');
    }
    
}

function preload(arrayOfImages) {
    $(arrayOfImages).each(function(){
        $('.preimg')[0].src = this;
        // Alternatively you could use:
        //(new Image()).src = this;
    });
}

function jumpToMiniProgram(id,sku){
    //id:(此参数填写产品id)
    console.log(id);
    wx.miniProgram.navigateTo({url: '/pages/goodsDetails/goodsDetails?productCode='+id+'&sku='+sku})
}

function getMeta(url, callback) {
    const img = new Image();
    img.src = url;
    img.onload = function() { callback(this.width, this.height); }
}

function subbundle_init(){}

function subb_mapmove(e:any){
    _lastRotation = e.rotation;
    if(imgnode.length > 1){
        keep_rotate();
    }
    if(imgnode.length > 0){
        if(imgnode[0].hasOwnProperty("obj3D")){
            if (e.mode == "mode.dollhouse"){
                if(!imgnode[0].obj3D.visible){
                    $.each(imgnode,function(k,v){
                        imgnode[k].obj3D.visible = true;
                    })
                }
                
            }else{
                if(imgnode[0].obj3D.visible){
                    $.each(imgnode,function(k,v){
                        imgnode[k].obj3D.visible = false;
                    })
                }
            }
            if(e.mode == "mode.inside"){
                if($('.doorh_title').length > 0){
                    $('.doorh_title').remove();
                    $('.doorh_bottom').remove();
                }
            }
        }
    }
    /*
    if(blackwallnode.hasOwnProperty("obj3D")){
        if (e.mode == "mode.inside") {
            blackwallnode.obj3D.visible = true;
        }else{
            blackwallnode.obj3D.visible = false;
        }
    }*/
    /*console.log(e.sweep)
    console.log(e.rotation)*/

}

function subb_sdkReady(){
    console.log("subb sdkready")
}

function subb_mapphasechange(e:any){
    if (e.phase == "appphase.playing"){
        Promise.all([
            _mpSdk.Scene.register('labelBox',labelFactory ),
            _mpSdk.Scene.register('black_wallBox',black_wallFactory)
    
        ]).then((e) => {
            doorh();
            _mpSdk.Mattertag.getData()
            .then((e) => {
                e.forEach(element => {
                    _mpSdk.Mattertag.editOpacity(element['sid'], 0);
                    _mpSdk.Mattertag.preventAction(element['sid'], {
                        opening: true,
                    });
                });
            });
        });
    }
}

async function add_label(){
    await _mpSdk.Scene.createNode()
      .then((node)=>{
        imgnode[label_pointer] = node;
        imgComponent[label_pointer] = imgnode[label_pointer].addComponent('labelBox');
        var position = label_json[label_pointer].posit;
        var rotation = label_json[label_pointer].rotation;
        var scale = label_json[label_pointer].scale;
        imgnode[label_pointer].obj3D.position.set(position.x,position.y,position.z);
        imgnode[label_pointer].obj3D.rotation.set(rotation.x,rotation.y,rotation.z);
        imgnode[label_pointer].obj3D.scale.set(scale.x,scale.y);
        imgnode[label_pointer].start();
        console.log("imgnode67")
        console.log(imgnode[label_pointer])
        if(label_pointer < label_json.length){
            label_pointer++;
            add_label();
        }
        
        //rotation_label()
    });
    
    
}

async function add_blackwall(){
    await _mpSdk.Scene.createNode()
      .then((node)=>{
        blackwallnode = node;
        var blackwallComponent = blackwallnode.addComponent('black_wallBox');
        var position = black_wall.posit;
        var rotation = black_wall.rotation;
        var scale = black_wall.scale;
        blackwallnode.obj3D.position.set(position.x,position.y,position.z);
        blackwallnode.obj3D.rotation.set(rotation.x,rotation.y,rotation.z);
        blackwallnode.obj3D.scale.set(scale.x,scale.y);
        blackwallnode.start();
        blackwallnode.obj3D.visible = false;
        console.log("imgnode67")
        console.log(blackwallnode)
        //rotation_label()
    });
    
    
}

async function rotation_label(){
    var _translate_node = await _mpSdk.Scene.createNode();
    var _translate_myControl = _translate_node.addComponent('mp.transformControls');
    _translate_node.start();

    
    _translate_myControl.inputs.visible = true;

    // Attach the model to the transform control
    _translate_myControl.inputs.selection = imgnode[label_pointer];

    // set 'translate' mode to position the selection.
    _translate_myControl.inputs.mode = "translate";
    setTimeout(function(){
        console.log(_translate_myControl.inputs)
    },1000)
    
}

function black_wallBox(this: any){
    this.events = {
        ["INTERACTION.CLICK"]: true,
        ["INTERACTION.HOVER"]: true,
      };
      
      this.inputs = {
        visible: false,
      };
    
      this.onInit = function() {
        var THREE = this.context.three;
        var loader = new THREE.TextureLoader();
        var texture = loader.load(black_wall.url);
        var geometry = new THREE.PlaneBufferGeometry(1, 1);
        var material_value:any =  { map: texture , transparent: true };
        
        material_value.side = THREE.DoubleSide;
        
  
        this.material = new THREE.MeshBasicMaterial( material_value );
        this.material.side = 2;
        var mesh = new THREE.Mesh( geometry, this.material );

        this.material.name = "black_wall";
        this.outputs.objectRoot = mesh;
  
        this.outputs.collider = mesh;
        this.outputs.objectRoot.name = "black_wall";

    };
  
    this.onEvent = function(type, data) {
        if(type == "INTERACTION.CLICK"){
            console.log("box click");
        }
        if(type == "INTERACTION.HOVER"){
            console.log(this.outputs.objectRoot)
        }
        
    }

    this.onInputsUpdated = function(previous) {
    };

    this.onTick = function(tickDelta) {
    }

    this.onDestroy = function() {
        this.material.dispose();
    };
}

function labelBox(){
    this.events = {
        ["INTERACTION.CLICK"]: true,
        ["INTERACTION.HOVER"]: true,
      };
      
      this.inputs = {
        visible: false,
      };
    
      this.onInit = function() {
        var THREE = this.context.three;
        var loader = new THREE.TextureLoader();
     
        if (!ct.getCookie(label_json[label_pointer].name)) {
            var texture = loader.load(label_json[label_pointer].url);
        }else{
            var light_url = label_json[label_pointer].url;
            light_url = light_url.split(".png")[0];
            light_url = light_url + "_light.png";
            var texture = loader.load(light_url);
            label_json[label_pointer].isenter = true;
        }

        var geometry = new THREE.PlaneBufferGeometry(1, 1);
        var material_value:any =  { map: texture , transparent: true };
        
        material_value.side = THREE.DoubleSide;
        
  
        this.material = new THREE.MeshBasicMaterial( material_value );
        this.material.side = 2;
        var mesh = new THREE.Mesh( geometry, this.material );

        this.material.name = "label";
        this.outputs.objectRoot = mesh;
  
        this.outputs.collider = mesh;
        this.outputs.objectRoot.name = label_pointer;
     
    };
  
    this.onEvent = function(type, data) {
      if(type == "INTERACTION.CLICK"){
        console.log("box click");
        console.log(data);
        console.log(this);
        console.log(this.outputs.objectRoot);
        //this.outputs.objectRoot.visible = false;
        label_selected = this.outputs.objectRoot.name;
        console.log(label_selected);
        var THREE = this.context.three;
        
        $.each(imgnode, function (k, v) {
            if(label_json.length > k){
                console.log(label_json[k]);
                console.log(v);
                if (label_json[k].isLight && !label_json[k].isenter) {
                    var labelLoader = new THREE.TextureLoader();
                    var label_mesh = v.obj3D.children[0].material;
                    var light_url = label_json[k].url;
                    label_mesh.map = labelLoader.load("" + light_url);
                    label_mesh.map.needsUpdate = true;
                    label_json[k].isLight = false;
                }
            }
            
        });
        var labelLoader = new THREE.TextureLoader();
        var label_mesh = this.material;
        var light_url = label_json[label_selected].url;
        light_url = light_url.split(".png")[0];
        light_url = light_url + "_light.png";
        label_mesh.map = labelLoader.load("" + light_url);
        label_mesh.map.needsUpdate = true;
        label_json[label_selected].isLight = true;
        $('.doorh_title p').eq(0).html(`${label_json[label_selected].name}`);
        $('.doorh_title p').eq(1).html(`${label_json[label_selected].isenter ? "房间已点亮" : "未探索"}`);
      }
      if(type == "INTERACTION.HOVER"){
        console.log(this.outputs.objectRoot)
      }
      
    }
  
    this.onInputsUpdated = function(previous) {
    };
  
    this.onTick = function(tickDelta) {
    }
  
    this.onDestroy = function() {
      this.material.dispose();
    };
  }

function labelFactory(){
    return new labelBox();
}

function black_wallFactory(){
    return new black_wallBox();
}

function doorh(){
    var doorh_div = `<div class="doorh_title">
    <p class="label_name">Objects Nomades</p>
    <p class="label_status">${ct.getCookie(label_json[0].name) ? "房间已点亮" : "未探索"}</p>
    <hr>
    </div>`;

    var doorh_bottom = `<div class="doorh_bottom">
    <p class="doorh_bottom_label">双指拖动可放大或翻转</p>
    <button class="doorh_bottom_btn">探索此房间</button>
    </div>`;
   
    var mode = _mpSdk.Mode.Mode.DOLLHOUSE;
    var position = { x: -46.26609048306841,
        y: 37.17803688926145,
        z: -33.714167458076524 };
    var rotation = {x: -20.739713151236963,
        y: -125.14983770194053 };
    var transition = _mpSdk.Sweep.Transition.FLY;
    var zoom = 5;
    _mpSdk.Mode.moveTo(mode, {
        position: position,
        rotation: rotation,
        transition: transition,
        zoom: zoom
    })
        .then(function (nextMode) {
        $('body').append(doorh_div);
        $('body').append(doorh_bottom);
        $('#container').css({"pointer-events":"all"});
        $('.doorh_bottom_btn').click(function(){
            console.log(label_selected);
            console.log(label_json[label_selected]);
            //ct.setCookie(label_json[label_selected].name,true,30)
            const transition = _mpSdk.Sweep.Transition.FLY;
            _mpSdk.Sweep.moveTo(label_json[label_selected].start_sweep,{
                rotation: label_json[label_selected].start_rotate,
                transition:transition
            }).then((sweep)=>{
            
            })
        });
        console.log('Arrived at new view mode ' + nextMode);
        add_label();
        //add_blackwall();
        remove_lav_loading();
    })["catch"](function (error) {
    
        remove_lav_loading();
        
    });
}

function keep_rotate() {
    var now_rotate = (_lastRotation.y / 180) * Math.PI;
    imgnode[0].obj3D.rotation.set(0, now_rotate, 0);
    imgnode[1].obj3D.rotation.set(0, now_rotate, 0);
    imgnode[2].obj3D.rotation.set(0, now_rotate, 0);
    imgnode[3].obj3D.rotation.set(0, now_rotate, 0);
    imgnode[4].obj3D.rotation.set(0, now_rotate, 0);
    imgnode[5].obj3D.rotation.set(0, now_rotate, 0);
    imgnode[6].obj3D.rotation.set(0, now_rotate, 0);
    imgnode[7].obj3D.rotation.set(0, now_rotate, 0);
}
